## NEW_YORK.TLC_YELLOW_TRIPS_2009
mta_tax: FLOAT | $0.50 MTA tax that is automatically triggered based on the metered rate in use
fare_amount: FLOAT | The time-and-distance fare calculated by the meter | eg=[11.7]

total_amount: FLOAT | The total amount charged to passengers. Does not include cash tips | eg=[12.7]
pickup_latitude: FLOAT | Latitude where the meter was engaged | eg=[40.784246, 40.750648]
imp_surcharge: FLOAT | $0.30 improvement surcharge assessed trips at the flag drop. The improvement surcharge began being levied in 2015.
passenger_count: NUMBER | The number of passengers in the vehicle. This is a driver-entered value. | eg=[1]
payment_type: TEXT | A numeric code signifying how the passenger paid for the trip. 1= Credit card 2= Cash 3= No charge 4= Dispute 5= Unknown 6= Voided trip | eg=["CASH", "CREDIT"]
trip_distance: FLOAT | The elapsed trip distance in miles reported by the taximeter. | eg=[4.2, 3.1]
extra: FLOAT | Miscellaneous extras and surcharges. Currently, this only includes the $0.50 and $1 rush hour and overnight charges. | eg=[1.0]
rate_code: NUMBER | The final rate code in effect at the end of the trip. 1= Standard rate 2=JFK 3=Newark 4=Nassau or Westchester 5=Negotiated fare 6=Group ride
tip_amount: FLOAT | Tip amount – This field is automatically populated for credit card tips. Cash tips are not included. | eg=[0.0]
pickup_longitude: FLOAT | Longitude where the meter was engaged. | eg=[-73.947404, -73.994473]

dropoff_latitude: FLOAT | Latitude where the meter was disengaged | eg=[40.739257, 40.721032]
store_and_fwd_flag: TEXT | This flag indicates whether the trip record was held in vehicle memory before sending to the vendor, aka “store and forward,” because the vehicle did not have a connection to the server. Y= store and forward trip N= not a store and forward trip | eg=[""]
dropoff_longitude: FLOAT | Longitude where the meter was disengaged. | eg=[-73.976707, -73.99362]
vendor_id: TEXT | A code indicating the TPEP provider that provided the record. 1= Creative Mobile Technologies, LLC; 2= VeriFone Inc | eg=["DDS"]

problems: TEXT | NULL | eg=["None"]

nta_name: TEXT | This is the NTA name corresponding to the neighborhood tabulation area from the 2010 US Census that the tree point falls into. | eg=["Queensboro Hill"]
trunk_wire: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a trunk problem caused by wires or rope wrapped around the trunk | eg=["No"]
tree_id: NUMBER | Unique identification number for each tree point | eg=[333516, 333724]
x_sp: FLOAT | X coordinate, in state plane. Units are feet. | eg=[1036561.78, 1036530.017]
stump_diam: NUMBER | Diameter of stump measured through the center, rounded to the nearest inch. | eg=[0]
block_id: NUMBER | Identifier linking each tree to the block in the blockface table/shapefile that it is mapped on. | eg=[310721, 310728]
state: TEXT | All features given value 'New York' | eg=["New York"]
brch_other: TEXT | Indicates the presence of other branch problems | eg=["No"]
zip_city: TEXT | City as derived from zipcode. This is often (but not always) the same as borough. | eg=["Flushing"]
cb_num: NUMBER | Community board in which tree point is located | eg=[407]
cncldist: NUMBER | Council district in which tree point is located | eg=[20]
user_type: TEXT | This field describes the category of user who collected this tree point's data. | eg=["NYC Parks Staff"]
trnk_light: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a trunk problem caused by lighting installed on the tree | eg=["No"]
address: TEXT | Nearest estimated address to tree | eg=["59-041 157 STREET", "59-030 157 STREET"]
spc_common: TEXT | Common name for species, e.g. "red maple" | eg=["American linden", "cherry"]
zipcode: NUMBER | Five-digit zipcode in which tree is located | eg=[11355]
root_grate: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a root problem caused by metal grates in tree bed | eg=["No"]
brch_shoe: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a branch problem caused by sneakers in the branches | eg=["No"]
nta: TEXT | This is the NTA Code corresponding to the neighborhood tabulation area from the 2010 US Census that the tree point falls into. | eg=["QN62"]
spc_latin: TEXT | Scientific name for species, e.g. "Acer rubrum" | eg=["Tilia americana", "Prunus"]
status: TEXT | Indicates whether the tree is alive, standing dead, or a stump. | eg=["Alive"]
steward: TEXT | Indicates the number of unique signs of stewardship observed for this tree. Not recorded for stumps or dead trees. | eg=["None"]
guards: TEXT | Indicates whether a guard is present, and if the user felt it was a helpful or harmful guard. Not recorded for dead trees and stumps | eg=["None"]
root_stone: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a root problem caused by paving stones in tree bed | eg=["No"]
sidewalk: TEXT | Indicates whether one of the sidewalk flags immediately adjacent to the tree was damaged, cracked, or lifted. Not recorded for dead trees and stumps. | eg=["NoDamage", "Damage"]
created_at: DATE | The date tree points were collected in the census software | eg=["2015-10-15", "2015-10-16"]
curb_loc: TEXT | Location of tree bed in relationship to the curb; trees are either along the curb (OnCurb) or offset from the curb (OffsetFromCurb) | eg=["OnCurb"]
latitude: FLOAT | Latitude of point, in decimal degrees | eg=[40.7394285, 40.73970209]
trnk_other: TEXT | Indicates the presence of other trunk problems | eg=["No"]
brch_light: TEXT | Indicates the presence of a branch problem caused by lights (usually string lights) or wires in the branches | eg=["No"]
tree_dbh: NUMBER | Diameter of the tree, measured at approximately 54" / 137cm above the ground. | eg=[2, 22]

status: TEXT | Excellent: full, well balanced crown and limb structure; leaves normal size color; no dead or broken branches; trunk solid; bark intact. Good: crown uneven or misshapen; some mechanical damage to bark or trunk; some signs of insects or disease; leaves somewhat below normal size and quantity; some dead or broken branches (less than half of the tree). Poor: large dead limbs with over one- half of the tree already dead or removed; large cavities; drastic deformities; leaves significantly below normal size and quantity; severe insect or disease damage. Dead: dead tree; leaves absent; twigs brittle. Shaft: all branches removed; trunk left standing; sprouts may or may not be evident. Stump: stump shorter than breast height; leaves entirely absent or present only on stump sprouts Empty pit: Pit contains exposed soil and no tree | eg=["Good", "Excellent"]

## NOAA_GSOD.GSOD1955
da: TEXT | The day | eg=["15", "27"]
snow_ice_pellets: TEXT | Indicators (1 = yes, 0 = no/not reported) for the occurrence during the day | eg=["0"]
wban: TEXT | WBAN number where applicable--this is the historical "Weather Bureau Air Force Navy" number - with WBAN being the acronym | eg=["99999"]
flag_prcp: TEXT | A = 1 report of 6-hour precipitation amount
B = Summation of 2 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
C = Summation of 3 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
D = Summation of 4 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
E = 1 report of 12-hour precipitation amount
F = Summation of 2 reports of 12-hour precipitation amount
G = 1 report of 24-hour precipitation amount
H = Station reported '0' as the amount for the day (eg, from 6-hour reports), but also reported at least one occurrence of precipitation in hourly observations--this could indicate a trace occurred, but should be considered as incomplete data for the day.
I = Station did not report any precip data for the day and did not report any occurrences of precipitation in its hourly observations--it's still possible that precip occurred but was not reported | eg=["H", "A"]
count_wdsp: TEXT | Number of observations used in calculating mean wind speed | eg=["4", "0"]
count_stp: NUMBER | Number of observations used in calculating mean station pressure | eg=[0, 4]
visib: FLOAT | Mean visibility for the day in miles to tenths.  Missing = 999.9 | eg=[18.8, 999.9]
count_temp: NUMBER | Number of observations used in calculating mean temperature | eg=[4]
hail: TEXT | Indicators (1 = yes, 0 = no/not reported) for the occurrence during the day | eg=["0"]

prcp: FLOAT | Total precipitation (rain and/or melted snow) reported during the day in inches and hundredths; will usually not end with the midnight observation--i.e., may include latter part of previous day. 
.00 indicates no measurable precipitation (includes a trace).
Missing = 99.99
Note: Many stations do not report '0' on days with no precipitation--therefore, '99.99' will often appear on these days. Also, for example, a station may only report a 6-hour amount for the period during which rain fell. See Flag field for source of data | eg=[99.99, 0.0]

flag_prcp: TEXT | A = 1 report of 6-hour precipitation amount
B = Summation of 2 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
C = Summation of 3 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
D = Summation of 4 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
E = 1 report of 12-hour precipitation amount
F = Summation of 2 reports of 12-hour precipitation amount
G = 1 report of 24-hour precipitation amount
H = Station reported '0' as the amount for the day (eg, from 6-hour reports), but also reported at least one occurrence of precipitation in hourly observations--this could indicate a trace occurred, but should be considered as incomplete data for the day.
I = Station did not report any precip data for the day and did not report any occurrences of precipitation in its hourly observations--it's still possible that precip occurred but was not reported | eg=["I", "A"]

year: TEXT | The year | eg=["1930"]
flag_prcp: TEXT | A = 1 report of 6-hour precipitation amount
B = Summation of 2 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
C = Summation of 3 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
D = Summation of 4 reports of 6-hour precipitation amount
E = 1 report of 12-hour precipitation amount
F = Summation of 2 reports of 12-hour precipitation amount
G = 1 report of 24-hour precipitation amount
H = Station reported '0' as the amount for the day (eg, from 6-hour reports), but also reported at least one occurrence of precipitation in hourly observations--this could indicate a trace occurred, but should be considered as incomplete data for the day.
I = Station did not report any precip data for the day and did not report any occurrences of precipitation in its hourly observations--it's still possible that precip occurred but was not reported | eg=["I"]
